***redenaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:redenaar.html>redenaar</a> (48603)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Redner</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:during.html>during</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> sixteenth <a href = vnd.unilang:century.html>century</a>.
</p>
